< Review>
For myself personally, 3636 club is the head cornerstone of dive bars in LB. I rate it 5 stars every time I go because of the friendly atmosphere, people and great service.I Definitely recommend it. this bar features Ricky's Tuesday night TACOS (check website for other nights as well) . A stand up regulation golden tee (current) and 2, yes 2! pool tables that are very well taken care of along side a working quarter change machine. Also a Touchtunes jukebox is generally always on unless of an event. And Please Drink Responsibly Thanks</Review>

<rating>5<//rating><text>-Cash only -No tap list -Inexpensive -Very cold bottles of beer || The best dive bar I've gotten to know. I avoided 36/36 for a long time but, to my surprise, I find it clean, well ventilated, spacious, and accommodating. Two bar-sized pool tables, a decent jukebox selection, never too loud. Inexpensive. Downsides are a lack of taps for beer, no proper ginger ale for ginger-related drinks. But, no one expected it to be perfect. If you walk in at all, you're not really going to care about a few missing ingredients or components; in fact - one would argue - this adds to the aesthetic of the place. Trust me on this one; if you're willing to go at all, you're going to accidentally end up loving it. PROTIP: There's a laundromat right next door; do some laundry, play some pool, grab a drink.</text><Pics>None<//Pics>< resp>

<userid>102311559299823270418< /userid><name>Alex Hasapis</name>< time>
1544403301294< /time>
<Rating>5<//Rating>< Text>
We have used Caliber Collision on Laurel Canyon Blvd. twice in the last seven months (don't ask).  The first time we did not use insurance.  The estimate we received was half of what a "highly recommended" shop gave us.  We received a clear and detailed explanation of what the work would involve and all our questions were answered patiently.  We were leaving town for a few days and there was no problem with the car being held for us after the work was done.  We received timely updates while were gone.  Upon returning to pick up the car we were truly amazed at the quality of the work.  There was absolutely no evidence of the damage or that any body work had been done.  Not only was the original large scrape  and hole in the bumper fixed, but a number of small scratches and scrapes were taken care of also.  we were sincerely amazed at the quality of the work.
Our second experience involved a small front end collision.  This was handled through Geico.  Since this location is an "ARX" (Auto Repair Express) center for Geico, the process was seamless.  We brought the car in and the Geico rep and the Caliber rep put together an estimate.  Again, everything was explained in detail, including deductible, payment  and repair work.  With ARX, a rental from Enterprise was waiting along with the Enterprise rep.  The whole process took about 45 minutes.  The work was completed as promised, actually a day early.  Once again, the repairs were flawless.
We highly recommend this location of Caliber Collision.  They are very professional and friendly.  Coming from NYC we know the difference.  We especially would like to thank Karen (manager), Mark (service advisor), and the always smiling Maria (office manager).<//Text>

<text>Visited Soup Shop a few weeks ago when we had a craving for some hot soup. Soup Shop is located in the big shopping Plaza with Target, Wells Fargo, Northgate Market, Game Stop. Due to COVID restrictions, they offer outdoor dining. They offer a large selection of dishes from wings, meat pies, noodles, rice, pho and boba drinks.

I ordered the chicken pho with chicken breast meat. You have the option of chicken breast or chicken thigh. I had my chicken pho with veggie broth, but you have the option of getting it with beef broth if you want a stronger meaty broth. The veggie broth was clear, flavorful and light.

Can't wait to go back to try their garlic fries.<//text></record>

< Name>
Joseph Chou< /Name>
<time>1583378388629<//time><rate>5<//rate>< Text>
Legit, this food is good. If you have a hankering for garlic noodles before, you either had to go to Nguyen's Kitchen on Main St. Or The Soup & Noodle on Tustin. Now this is in such a convenient area!!

The fried rice is very unique, as they add some coconut milk for some creaminess to pair with the savory aspect.

The garlic noodles are very garlicky, so as a garlic lover, it's perfect! I had it paired with the shaken beef and the meat was seasoned very well, really savory with a tinge of sweetness. My friend had the ribs with his and legit it was super soft and fell off the bone.

The pho is great too, very clean and natural tasting, without the usual over the top beef flavors some pho restaurants add.

Overall, excellent little place! Would highly recommend!<//Text>

<user_id>115557746769841414552</user_id><username>B. P.< /username><date>1584225143806<//date>< rate>
5< /rate>
< Review>
Good on the budget, tasty, memorable, family owned.

Looking for a way to warm up while leaving satisfied, stomach and wallet? Seek no further because Soup Shop is your stop for all this. Firstly, you walk in and get this excited feeling. Being a small spot you get a clear view of the restaurant. Good sized tables that can accommodate any customer(s) that walk in. First come first serve (unless you reserve a table), and come fast because I can tell they get busy at night.

Walking in you already get a good vibe about the place. You will be kindly seated by one of the servers of the restaurant, which is one of the daughters. I'm given a menu with my Pho, appetizer, and drink options. Staff members have no problems answering questions, and give their best recommendations. Fast paced workers with great attitudes. This Pho location is great for coming alone, or spending time with friends and family.

Signature key ingredients, enticing broth that simmers for 24-hours- the list could go for reasons to go back. Ordering oxtail with beef rib was new and needed. A mixture of this soothing broth, green onion, white onion, soft noodles, and tender meat will have you craving for more. I awaited every spoonful. Very appetizing overall.

I also enjoyed the "Crunchy Pork Bao", first experience trying quail egg- and the sweetness of the pork shoulder gave it a nice flavor. The drink options all sound tasty, I ordered however the Jasmine Honey Green Tea. This drink was refreshing after the hearty soup. If you're looking for something to cleanse your pallet that coincides with your meal, I recommend it. In the end, this is an experience for food lovers and newcomers to the Pho scene.

I'll be back.

-B.P.<//Review>

<Text>I've seen Blue Water Seafood & Crab many times while driving down Willow St. I decided to make a pit stop there for the first time to grab some lunch. I definitely thought it was cool bar and grill for casual hangouts and watching games. It was a football Sunday too, so they had Red Zone on all the TVs.

I found a seat at the bar and was greeted promptly by one of the bartenders. Customer service was excellent all around. My food came out super fast, and the bartender was awesome. She was friendly and attentive as she would frequently check up on me. I appreciated that she knew her all regulars very well, which gave me the sense of community and camaraderie at Blue Water Seafood & Crab.

I ordered the soft shell crab sandwich with a side of cajun fries. It was a solid sandwich. It would've been very plain If it wasn't for the cajun crab flavored aioli in the sandwich. I liked that they used a brioche type of bun - nice and soft but held everything together well. The fries were decent. They were mostly limp, so it would've been nice if they could've been cooked longer. I also felt like they were sitting out for a bit, because I got them barely warm.
